< review>
Fantastic, elegant, highline Vietnamese cuisine, and also Pho. 35 years in Encinitas, same family, fantastic food the whole time.
If you haven't tried Vietnamese food, this is where you should go to start. Ask for suggestions and prepare to be amazed.
If you have learned to love Vietnamese food, this is where you should go to get more. Ask for suggestions and prepare to be amazed.</review>

<text>The key point about Kim's is that they adapt traditional Vietnamese cuisine for healthy eating. For example, they offer steamed spring rolls in addition to the traditional fried spring rolls; they offer brown rice in addition to the traditional white rice; the lemon grass wrap is packed with raw, fresh veggies; and so on. It's a little expensive considering the ambiance, but it does fill a niche for health conscience people who want Vietnamese food.<//text><pics>None<//pics>< resp>

< Review>
Great place to eat in the Frazier Park area. Worth the small detour off the 5 freeway if you‚Äôre passing through. Good selection of food, extremely friendly staff, fun decor and seating areas, live music upstairs. You will pay slightly more than other places in Frazier, but it‚Äôs worth it. House made sodas compliment their meals nicely. They roast their own coffee and have bags for purchase. My only small issue was the coffee - I would have liked it to have more developed flavors for being freshly roasted. But still, a great little restaurant overall. If I‚Äôm ever in the area again, I‚Äôll come here.< /Review>

< review>
This restaurant started from a food truck. Now it's found a permanent home in Pomona. Chef is taiwanese, food was mixture of asian influence, easy finger food that's gourmet. Was able to try top selling items for the last 8 years. Tasted lobster corndog, hamachi tartare taco. This was my favorite. All the sliders were great kobe beef slider, pork belly asian style slider. The meat melts in ur mouth. The fried oyster taco was interesting and different. Walnut shrimp taco was another favorite. They have spring rolls here too, will come back and try other breakfast and lunch items.<//review>

< Text>
This is probably my favorite restaurant in the whole city. If you don't know this restaurant you go there for Americanized tourist food. But if you know, you go there for one thing and one thing only--clay pot rice. My favorite is the one with sausages and smoked ham. And I'll tell you a secret: after you finish the rice, tell them to make a soup for you with the leftover rice stuck to the clay pot sides.
I've had same dish in China and Hong Kong and nothing compares. I've had this since the current owner's mom was making it. It's still the best I've ever had.< /Text>

<Text>Guys, this is not a place for dim sum, orange chicken, spicy and sour soup.  This is a truly Cantonese Chinese restaurant; they are good at home/village food.  They don't make dim sum here.  The dim sum are brought from next door (surprise to hear it is microwave or frozen; never ever had this issue before).  What you should order here are steam live fish, clay pot rice, etc. Go with a Chinese friend.  The English level here is low, so miscommunication is bound to happen.  My parents only liked eating here and so my family eat here when we go to Chinatown; we have been coming here for over 20 years.  Never had an issue but I have witnessed frustrated customers because they did not know what to order and the waitress were awkward.  But since I understand how their body language can be misunderstood, so I understand all the negative experience as described here.  And they are extremely understaffed.  If I were you expecting spring roll and dim sum and in a rush and attentive service, don't come here.  If you are not judgmental about eating fish with a head on and don't mind the floor is sticky, and water may spilled out by accident, the food is great, if you know what to order.  $60 for 3 people is not expensive in SF.  They only accept cash.  I give a 3 star for lack of polish in service.  The food deserves a 4.<//Text><username>Alinna Lee<//username><Time>1474067212534< /Time></record></dataset><record>

<username>Mari M<//username><Time>1565586268496< /Time><rate>4<//rate><Review>Sol Cubano is like a little hole in the wall burst of flavor. It literally is the only caribbean restaurant in Sacramento. If only we had more like Miami but who am I kidding :o .. I do love the dinner plate Ropa Vieja,(shredded beef in a sauce) however, the times I've come it has tasted different each time. Some really good, some not the greatest. So I have now been ordering the Carne de Res con papa (beef chunks with potatoes) so far so good. I always order an order of Tostones (fried green plaintains) y Maduros (fried sweet plaintains)  & my dinner always ends with a Cortado ( cuban espresso) & un pastellito de guayaba (guava pastry). Being a Puerto Rican/Cuban in Sacramento is so hard because there literally are NO restaurants with our food. So when I am feeling homesick I always drop in! Give it a try! The downfall is they are ONLY OPEN 4days/wk (Wednesday-Saturday)

<review>Never did come to a completely amicable conclusion here, so I will still recommend going elsewhere.

Final Update:
I received a call from Nissan Corporate this morning, and unfortunately they will not be able to help, as they will take the dealer's side on this.  The issue is, the dealer is communicating my concern to them incorrectly.  And even when I tried to explain to Nissan Corporate, they will defer to what the dealership is saying.  Oh well.  I cannot recommend anyone shop here for anything.  These situations are probably only going to resolve themselves with class action litigation.  Just Beware!

Update:
I received a call from the dealership saying that the scratches were fixed, along with the dents. The area that was scratched does look repaired. That's great. Unfortunately, the dents that they claimed were fixed are mostly fixed, except for the largest and most obvious one to see. Needless to say, I will be contacting Nissan corporate tomorrow, and likely filing a complaint with the Bureau of Automotive Repairs. Nobody should endure this type of runaround when they purchase a new car. I have not had my van for more than half of the time I've owned it over the last 3 weeks. This is just unacceptable. With that said, everyone at the dealership has been very nice, including Liza and Evan. I'm not sure who "Nathan" is, that the manager mentioned in his response to my review here.

I would stay away from here at all costs. They say one thing to your face, but they don't respect you at all. We purchased a brand new 2019 NV Passenger from them on April 21st. We purchased the perma plate option, for paint and exterior protection as well, because it's always nice to have extra coverage. Fast forward to today, and I have had the car at the dealership since Monday, waiting for the "sales team" to decide what they want to do with a bunch of dings and a couple of deep (to the metal) scratches. I don't understand why my vehicle's fate is in the hands of sales people, but it is. I will be calling corporate promptly, but I want everyone to know that you better keep your guard up here. Do not accept any of their sales tactics as truth.

An honest review means a lot to me and I think it helps any business or organization to achieve it ultimate goal. Also from the customer perspective, a review helps others to understand what they are likely to expect. Here is my review for Ocean Nissan based on my recent business with them

Sales Department
----------------

1. No one was pushy (A typical sales style that possibly most hate).

2. Right from the moment you park your car and step in, people are happy to see you and willing  to help you. Always expect a big smile from most of them.

3. Hooman Keyvan is an amazing person and man who sticks to his words.. Always a winner for me in any profession. If you want your next Nissan talk to him. A genuine person.

4. The Sales Management team is very good and would tell you what they can and what they cannot do.

Service Department
------------------

1. The service department was responsible for applying the Enviroguard and they took some time as a loaner was available.

2. They service quality was good and I am hoping to get outstanding service as I step in to get my servicing in the future done.

3. I wish they have more loaner, so that customers donot need to wait for longer to get their work done.

Dealership
-------------

1. Clean and nice ambiance.

2. I heard that the owners visit it regularly and that I am sure shows their passion in the business.

3. Good selection of vehicles to choose from.

4. Car Doc and Enviroguard are good options that not many dealerships provide.
